> tanto := proc( k, d )
>   local sq, c, aa, c_b, i, n, a, b, f, para, nn, pp;
>   sq := evalf( sqrt( k ) );
>   print( k, sq );
>   c := ( (k*sqrt(k))/(p*sqrt(k)-(2*k)) ) * 2 ;
>   aa  := ( k / ( k - sq ) );
>   c_b := frac(k/aa) + d;
>   i := (k/c_b);
>   print( i );
>   n := c=i;
>   f := solve(n,p);
>   a := sqrt(k)/(f*sqrt(k)-(2*k));
>   b := 1-(f*sqrt(k))/(f*sqrt(k)-(2*k));
>   c := (k*sqrt(k))/(f*sqrt(k)-(2*k));
>   para := a*x^2+b*x+c=y;
>   parabola( P, para, [x,y] );
>   line( Y, y=x, [x,y] );
> 
>   point(K,k,0);
>   point(KK,k,k);
>   point(SQ,sq,sq);
>   point(SQ0,sq,0);
> 
>   line(A,[K,SQ]);
>   line(B,[KK,SQ0]);
> 
>   intersection(A3,A,B);
> 
>   line(C,[point(PC,0,i),A3]);
> 
>   print( solve( {Equation(P), Equation(Y)} ) );
>   print( solve( {Equation(P), y=sq} ) );
>   print( Equation(C), slope(C) );
>   print( solve( {Equation(C), x=0} ) );
>   print( solve( {Equation(C), y=0} ) );
>   print( solve( {Equation(P), Equation(C)} ) );
>   nn := solve( {Equation(C), Equation(Y)} );   print( rhs(nn[1]), convert(rhs(nn[1]),rational,10)  );
>   print("----------");
>   draw([Y,P(colour=green),C(colour=blue)],axes=normal,colour=black,view=[-k..k,-k..k]);
> 
> end proc:
